name:A‚Äçn‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçy‚Äçm‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçs‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Suite With Sea View

info:1 Review

posted:Posted August 17, 2021
msg:I stayed at this hotel 5 years ago, and I feel value for money. When I went to Xichang for a vacation and chose a hotel this time, I was almost discouraged when I saw the bad feedback about this hotel in the comment section, because I often go to Xichang and I have something to do with better hotels in the local area. Knowing a little, after careful consideration, he chose Baiyue. Fortunately, I made the right choice. The quality of the staff is quite high: the front desk staff are very attentive and take the initiative to consider the guests. When we saw our one and two children (two 14-year-old children) took the initiative to add a free breakfast for us, we temporarily increased our stay for one night. The room we stayed in has been booked, and the front desk staff took the trouble to watch them one by one until we were satisfied; the aunts who cleaned the room were very polite, and when they met in the corridors, they always greeted them warmly; the staff at breakfast was always enthusiastic Actively solve problems for guests. Hotel services are seamlessly connected: we only need to check in at the front desk, drive in and out of the gate, and let it go automatically without showing any voucher. We just need to take the temperature when we come back (this should be); we forget to bring a mask when we eat in the morning, and we have to prepare at the front desk when we eat. There are plenty of medical masks for guests to use for free. The old condition of the room facilities is not as serious as the reviews say, clean and tidy, even the infrequent storage partitions are very clean. The environment of the hotel has nothing to say. It is connected to the Huanhu Road and cannot go out when it rains. Sitting on the balcony and looking at the lake is also a kind of enjoyment. The barbecue in the hotel must be tasted, the taste is very good, if you only eat barbecue, you really don't need to go out of the hotel. A complete vacation.
[Living with a baby in love]

msg:When I searched the guide on Xiaohongshu, I found that many families with children choose Baiyue, so I ordered the cheapest apar**ent building for three consecutive nights, but the price/performance ratio was beyond imagination. It feels like being in Sanya. The balcony is of good size. You can do homework, watch the sea, dry your clothes, and exercise. The room is separated from dry and wet, convenient storage, and comfortable bedding. The breakfast is very rich and the dishes are fresh. The room service attitude is super good. Drinks are delivered every night and fruits are delivered in the afternoon. The cleaning sisters are very warm and friendly. The hotel swimming pool is free, you can see the sea and the scenery, which feels like Thailand. The hotel is right on the Qionghai Sea. Because the scenery is so beautiful, we walked directly from the hotel along the Qionghai Sea for two days. Dinner is also eaten in the hotel, which is actually cheaper than outside. When I went home and found that I had lost something, the hotel immediately found the courier. Very good five-star environment and service.
